I lead the engineering of Quantum Link ╬®-3.0.0, a Unified Sovereign Platform engineered for maximum autonomy across devices and environments.

My work focuses on Bio-Entanglement pipelines, Digital Twin engines, and AI governance systems that let users own their compute.
